        function UniversalDataLayer(udl) {

              return this._data[key];
            }

            });

  <script>
   function getQueryParam(paramName) {
        var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
        var params = query.split('&');
        for (var i = 0; i < params.length; i += 1) {
          var pair = params[i].split('=');
          if (pair[0] === paramName) {
            return pair[1];
          }
        }
        return false;
      };
      function removeURLParameter(url, param) {
        var urlParts = url.split('?');
        if (urlParts.length >= 2) {
          var prefix = "".concat(encodeURIComponent(param), "=");
          var params = urlParts[1].split(/[&;]/g);
          for (var i = params.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
            if (params[i].lastIndexOf(prefix, 0) !== -1) {
              params.splice(i, 1);
            }
          }
          url = urlParts[0];
          if (params.length > 0) {
            url += "?".concat(params.join('&'));
          }
          return url;
        }
        return url;
      };
      function setCookie(cookieName, value, daysToExpire) {
        var expires = '';
        if (daysToExpire) {
          var date = new Date();
          date.setTime(date.getTime() + daysToExpire * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
          expires = "; expires=".concat(date.toGMTString());
        }
        if (expires !== '') {
          document.cookie = "".concat(cookieName, "=").concat(value).concat(expires, "; path=/");
        }
        return true;
      };
      (function(){
        var hid = getQueryParam('hid');
        if (!hid) {
          return;
        }
        setCookie('hid', hid, 90);
        window.location.replace(removeURLParameter(window.location.href, 'hid'));
      })();
  </script>

   window.mdp = window.mdp || {};
      window.mdp.getCookieValue = function getCookieValue(name) {
        var cookie = document.cookie.match('(^|;)\\s*' + name + '\\s*=\\s*([^;]+)');
        return cookie ? decodeURIComponent(cookie.pop()) : '';
      }

             <div class="media-body article-info bucket-margin margin-24-bottom clearfix">
              <h4 class="headline">
               <a class="heading-3 heading-content margin-8-bottom media-heading headline" data-tracking-label="Dinner Recipes &gt; What Is Detroit-Style Pizza and How Do You Make It at Home?" href="https://www.allrecipes.com/article/what-is-detroit-style-pizza-and-how-do-you-make-it-at-home/">
                What Is Detroit-Style Pizza and How Do You Make It at Home?
               </a>
              </h4>
              <span class="summary margin-8-bottom">
               Pizza can look and taste very different depending on where you're from or what kind of pie you prefer. Neapolitan-style, New York-style, and Chicago deep-dish are all very popular pizzas nationwide, but have you heard of Detroit-style pizza? Ask anyone from Michigan and this is the pizza they have been devouring for decades. Read on to learn about Detroit-style pizza and how to make it at home.
              </span>
             </div>
            </div>
            <ul aria-labelledby="submenu-label-3" class="submenu-children featured-content">
             <li class="menu-item-main heading-menu">
              <a class="submenu-link child-link" data-tracking-label="dinner recipes &gt; dinner fix" href="https://www.allrecipes.com/kitchen-tips/how-to/dinner-fix/">
               Dinner Fix

              <h4 class="headline">
               <a class="heading-3 heading-content margin-8-bottom media-heading headline" data-tracking-label="Kitchen Tips &gt; How to Clean Dirty Sheet Pans" href="https://www.allrecipes.com/article/how-to-clean-sheet-pans/">
                How to Clean Dirty Sheet Pans
               </a>
              </h4>
              <span class="summary margin-8-bottom">
               Learn the best ways to clean a dirty sheet pan and keep it clean. Use baking soda and vinegar, dryer sheets, or hydrogen peroxide and baking soda to clean your sheet pans.
